<div class="articleWide cleared">
  <div class="alpha">
    <div id="js-article-text" class="article-text wide">
        <h1>'It was easy': Man, 26, who shot dead his 24-year-old co-worker the day after he was fired told police she ruined his life - as he appears in shackled in court wearing anti-suicide smock</h1>
<ul class="mol-bullets-with-font"><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>Christopher O'Kroley, 26, is accused of shooting dead 24-year-old Caroline Nosal at Metro Market Cottage Grove in Madison, Wisconsin, on Tuesday</strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>O'Kroley had been fired from the market on Monday, two weeks after Nosal accused him of </strong></font><span style="font-size: 16.8px;"><b>harassment</b></span></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>Coworkers described the relationship between O'Kroley and Nosal, of Stoughton, as one that soured after O'Kroley 'wanted more'</strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>Nosal died of gunshot wounds to the head and abdomen, an autopsy said</strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>O'Kroley's bond was set at $1million on Friday after he was pushed into the courtroom in a wheelchair while wearing a suicide-prevention smock </strong></font></li><li class=""><span style="font-size: 16.8px;"><b>He was charged with first-degree intentional homicide and first-degree reckless endangerment</b></span></li></ul><p class="author-section byline-plain">By

<a href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Kelly+Mclaughlin+For+Dailymail.com" class="author" rel="nofollow">Kelly Mclaughlin For Dailymail.com</a>


</p>
<p class="byline-section"><span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-published">

</p><div itemprop="articleBody"><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">A Wisconsin man was charged with first-degree intentional homicide on Friday after he allegedly killed one of his former coworkers in the parking lot of the market where they both worked. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Christopher O'Kroley, 26, is accused of shooting dead 24-year-old Caroline Nosal at Metro Market Cottage Grove in Madison on Tuesday, a day after he was fired from his job. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em"></font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Coworkers described the relationship between O'Kroley and Nosal, of Stoughton, as one that soured after O'Kroley 'wanted more'. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">O'Kroley's bond was set at $1million on Friday after he was pushed into the courtroom in a wheelchair while wearing a suicide-prevention smock, according to <a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="" rel="nofollow" href="http://www.wkow.com/story/31152274/2016/02/05/police-okroley-confesses-cites-firing-as-homicide-motive">WKOW</a>. An anti-suicide smock is a tear-resistant noose-proof form of clothing that officials put detainees in if they are on suicide watch.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">He was also charged with first-degree reckless endangerment.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em"><span class="mol-style-bold">Scroll down for video </span></font></p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group">    <div class="mol-img">  <img id="i-c8af2f93387c6916" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/02/06/04/30EBD46A00000578-3434586-image-a-70_1454734229156.jpg" height="454" width="634" alt="Christopher O'Kroley, 26, is accused of shooting dead 24-year-old Caroline Nosal at Metro Market Cottage Grove in Madison, Wisconsin, on Tuesday. He is pictured in an anti-suicide smock, being wheeled into the courtroom on Friday" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
</div>    <p class="imageCaption">Christopher O'Kroley, 26, is accused of shooting dead 24-year-old Caroline Nosal at Metro Market Cottage Grove in Madison, Wisconsin, on Tuesday. He is pictured in an anti-suicide smock, being wheeled into the courtroom on Friday</p></div><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group">    <div class="mol-img">  <img id="i-9bba7ad8403374b2" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/02/06/04/30EBD7D400000578-3434586-image-a-71_1454734232958.jpg" height="429" width="634" alt="O'Kroley's bond was set at $1million on Friday after he was charged with first-degree intentional homicide" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
</div>    <p class="imageCaption">O'Kroley's bond was set at $1million on Friday after he was charged with first-degree intentional homicide</p></div><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group"><div class="mol-img">  <img id="i-7eb75de18bee5f19" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/02/06/05/30ED553E00000578-3434586-image-a-34_1454736967503.jpg" height="510" width="634" alt="Nosal, 24 (seen in a Facebook picture), died of gunshot wounds to the head and abdomen, an autopsy said. Coworkers described the relationship between O'Kroley and Nosal, of Stoughton, as one that soured" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
</div><div class="clear"></div><p class="imageCaption">Nosal, 24 (seen in a Facebook picture), died of gunshot wounds to the head and abdomen, an autopsy said. Coworkers described the relationship between O'Kroley and Nosal, of Stoughton, as one that soured</p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Two weeks before the shooting, O'Kroley was suspended from work after Nosal told a store manager that she was being harassed by him. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">O'Kroley told police that following his suspension, he began planning to kill Nosal and himself if he was fired, according to the <a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="" rel="nofollow" href="http://host.madison.com/wsj/news/local/crime-and-courts/christopher-o-kroley-charged-with-murder-for-metro-market-shooting/article_47990e9b-b6b9-5279-bf6f-fdd1e4494ac5.html">Wisconsin State Journal</a>.  </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span style="font-size: 14.4px;">He also told police when he was arrested on Wednesday that he would have shot Nosal to death a day earlier but he wanted to practice shooting the gun he had bought Monday before using it. </span></p><div><div class="related-carousel with-fb news"
     id="p-20"

So O'Kroley went home, watched movies and ordered pizza before returning the next day to attempt the shooting again, police said. </span></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span style="font-size: 14.4px;">He returned to the market on Tuesday and shot Nodal in the head and abdomen as she walked through the parking lot as she left work, a criminal complaint said. </span></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span style="font-size: 14.4px;">O'Kroley had learned through former co-workers via text message - on the pretext of collecting his belongings from the store when Nosal was not there - that Nosal finished work at 8pm on Tuesday. </span></p><div class="moduleFull mol-video"><a name="video" class="namedLink"></a><div class="item">

</div></div><div class="splitRight"><div class="mol-img">  <img id="i-3b5cb457c936bf5a" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/02/06/05/30ED551A00000578-3434586-image-m-38_1454736991470.jpg" height="402" width="306" alt="But after the shooting of Nosal, he realized that he couldn't kill himself, he told police" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
</div></div><div class="clear"></div><p class="imageCaption">O'Kroley said he planned to kill Nosal and himself if he was fired from Metro Market after his suspension. But after the shooting, he realized that he couldn't kill himself, he told police. Nosal is pictured above on Facebook</p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span style="font-size: 14.4px;">He told police that he knelt down beside her car, and when he saw Nosal turn the corner, he stood up and shot at her chest. </span></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span style="font-size: 14.4px;">When she fell, he shot her once more in the head, he told police. </span></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span style="font-size: 14.4px;">He said that it was 'easy' to kill Nosal because she had 'ruined my life', and that he killed her out of anger. He described himself to police as a 'sociopath'.  </span></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">'I killed Caroline and I'm about to kill myself. So don't be surprised when I don't respond anymore,' O'Kroley wrote in a text message to a coworker after the shooting. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">But he realized that he couldn't kill himself, he told police, and that his plan was to 'hijack someone's car at gunpoint', but he instead fled the scene in his own car.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">O'Kroley was arrested on Wednesday about four miles from an area where his car was found abandoned. Police used K9s and a drone to search for him, according to <a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="" rel="nofollow" href="http://www.channel3000.com/news/okroley-was-fired-from-grocery-store-blamed-nosal-for-complaint/37840446">Channel 3000</a>.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">He exchanged gunfire with Madison Police Officer Michele Walker before he was arrested, which led to a first-degree reckless endangerment charge on Friday.  </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">'I'm glad I didn't hit her,' he said in court of firing at the officer twice. 'I don't know what else, I guess I'm sorry but... I don't know if I am sorry, I'm just glad I didn't hit her.' </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Madison police spokesman Joel DeSpain said the department believes that O'Kroley 'purchased the firearm locally and legally at a store, however that part of the investigation is still ongoing'. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Wisconsin Legislature eliminated a 48-hour waiting period for purchasing a handgun last year. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">A former girlfriend of O'Kroley told the Wisconsin State Journal that he had been mentally ill for the past decade and tried to commit suicide in 2014.  </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em"></font></p></div>

<script async src="//cdn.taboola.com/libtrc/dailymail-us/loader.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    DM.later('bundle', function(){
        var n = 0;
        var taboola_every_n = 10;
        var taboola_counter = 10;

        var addTaboola = function (node){
            var id = "taboola-stream-thumbnails-" + (++n);
            var taboola_node = '<div id="' + id + '" style="min-height: 280px;"></div>';
            $(node).before(taboola_node);

            window._taboola = window._taboola || [];
            _taboola.push({
                mode: 'thumbnails-b',
                container: id,
                placement: "Stream Thumbnails " + n});
        };

        DM.has('infinite-list', 'InfiniteList', {
url: '/api/infinite-list.html?channelShortName=news&pageSize=10',
            total: 20.0,
            from: 0,
            onAfterAppend: function (container){
                var items = $(container).children('div');
                if(!taboola_every_n){
                    return;
                }

                items.each(function (){
                    if (taboola_counter == 0){
                        addTaboola(this);
                        taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;
                    }
                    else {
                        taboola_counter--;
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    });
</script>
